method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  // Soundness: every element in result is a possible line
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  // Completeness: every possible line appears in result
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)

    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];

            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {

            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])

        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{

  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }

ghost predicate InSeq(x: int, s: seq<int>)
{
  exists i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == x
}

ghost predicate PossibleLine(line: int, stops: seq<seq<int>>)
{
  forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: InSeq(line, stops[k])
}

lemma InSeqExtend(x: int, s: seq<int>, y: int)
  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])
{
  var w :| 0 <= w < |s| && s[w] == x;
  assert (s + [y])[w] == x;
}

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert newResult[w] == result[idx];
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert newResult[|newResult|-1] == result[i];
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], oldNR + [result[i]]);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    // (No explicit proof required; the invariant ensures it)

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

  // Soundness: every element in result is a possible line
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  // Completeness: every possible line appears in result

      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) == InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result) == InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)

          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)

              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {

            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }

        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    // (No explicit proof needed; the invariant ensures completeness)

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert newResult[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(newResult[w], stops[k]);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert newResult[|oldNR|] == result[i];
              assert InSeq(newResult[|oldNR|], stops[k]);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)

    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {

      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) == InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Invariant 2 for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              // oldNR already contains result[idx]
            }
          } else { // idx == i
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              // result[i] is appended to newResult
            }
          }
        }
        // Invariant 1 for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])

      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    // (No additional assertions needed; the loop invariant already guarantees it.)

    result := newResult;
  }

  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }

ghost predicate InSeq(x: int, s: seq<int>)
{
  exists i | 0 <= i < |s| :: s[i] == x
}

ghost predicate PossibleLine(line: int, stops: seq<seq<int>>)
{
  forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: InSeq(line, stops[k])
}

lemma InSeqExtend(x: int, s: seq<int>, y: int)
  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])
{
  var w :| 0 <= w < |s| && s[w] == x;
  assert (s + [y])[w] == x;
}

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}

lemma InSeqExtend(x: int, s: seq<int>, y: int)
  requires InSeq(x, s)
  ensures InSeq(x, s + [y])
{
  var w :| 0 <= w < |s| && s[w] == x;

method DetermineLine(stops: seq<seq<int>>) returns (result: seq<int>)
  ensures forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: PossibleLine(result[i], stops)
  ensures forall k | 0 <= k < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], result)
{
  if |stops| == 0 { result := []; return; }
  result := stops[0];
  for k := 1 to |stops|
    invariant forall i | 0 <= i < |result| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(result[i], stops[m])
    invariant forall x :: (forall m | 0 <= m < k :: InSeq(x, stops[m])) ==> InSeq(x, result)
  {
    var newResult: seq<int> := [];
    for i := 0 to |result|
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < |newResult| :: InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
      invariant forall idx | 0 <= idx < i :: InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
    {
      var found := false;
      for j := 0 to |stops[k]|
        invariant found <==> exists j' | 0 <= j' < j :: result[i] == stops[k][j']
      {
        if result[i] == stops[k][j] {
          found := true;
        }
      }
      if found {
        ghost var oldNR := newResult;
        newResult := newResult + [result[i]];
        // Prove invariant 2 is maintained for all idx < i+1
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < i + 1
          ensures InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) ==> InSeq(result[idx], newResult)
        {
          if idx < i {
            if InSeq(result[idx], stops[k]) {
              // oldNR already contains result[idx] by invariant
              assert InSeq(result[idx], oldNR);
              var w :| 0 <= w < |oldNR| && oldNR[w] == result[idx];
              // Thus it remains in newResult
              assert InSeq(result[idx], newResult);
            }
          } else {
            // idx == i, result[i] is last element of newResult
            if InSeq(result[i], stops[k]) {
              assert result[i] == newResult[|newResult|-1];
              assert InSeq(result[i], newResult);
            }
          }
        }
        // Prove invariant 1 is maintained for old elements
        forall idx | 0 <= idx < |oldNR|
          ensures InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result)
        {
          assert newResult[idx] == oldNR[idx];
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], stops[k]);
          assert InSeq(oldNR[idx], result);
          assert InSeq(newResult[idx], stops[k]) && InSeq(newResult[idx], result);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove soundness for next iteration
    assert forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult| :: forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
    by {
      forall i | 0 <= i < |newResult|
        ensures forall m | 0 <= m < k + 1 :: InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
      {
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], stops[k]);
        assert InSeq(newResult[i], result);
        var ridx :| 0 <= ridx < |result| && result[ridx] == newResult[i];
        forall m | 0 <= m < k
          ensures InSeq(newResult[i], stops[m])
        {
          assert InSeq(result[ridx], stops[m]);
        }
      }
    }

    // Prove completeness for next iteration
    assert forall k2 | 0 <= k2 < |stops| :: forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k2]| ::
            PossibleLine(stops[k2][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k2][j], newResult)
    by {
      forall k2 | 0 <= k2 < |stops|
        ensures forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k2]| ::
                PossibleLine(stops[k2][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k2][j], newResult)
      {
        assert k2 <= k;
        if k2 < k {
          // For lines seen earlier, completeness holds from invariant
          assert forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k2]| ::
                  PossibleLine(stops[k2][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k2][j], result);
          assert forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k2]| ::
                  PossibleLine(stops[k2][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k2][j], newResult);
        } else { // k2 == k
          // All lines in stops[k] that are possible appear in newResult
          assert forall j | 0 <= j < |stops[k]| ::
                  PossibleLine(stops[k][j], stops) ==> InSeq(stops[k][j], newResult);
        }
      }
    }

    result := newResult;
  }
}

method SameElements(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (same: bool)
{
  if |a| != |b| { return false; }
  for i := 0 to |a| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |b| {
      if a[i] == b[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  for i := 0 to |b| {
    var found := false;
    for j := 0 to |a| {
      if b[i] == a[j] { found := true; }
    }
    if !found { return false; }
  }
  return true;
}
